|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-537">EDI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-537">EDI</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-538">请参阅“电子数据交换 (EDI)”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-538">See electronic data interchange (EDI).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-539">EDIFACT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-539">EDIFACT</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-540">请参阅“用于管理、商务和贸易的电子数据交换 (EDIFACT)”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-540">See Electronic Data Interchange for Administration, Commerce and Trade (EDIFACT).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-541">EDIFACT UNOA 语法 (EDIFACT UNOA syntax)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-541">EDIFACT UNOA syntax</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-542">允许以下 EDIFACT 语法仅字符： 大写字母、 所有数字为空，感叹号 （！）、 引号 （"）、 百分比符号 （%），& 符 (&)、 左括号和右括号 （"（"和"）"），星号 （*）、 逗号、 短划线 （-）十进制点 （.）、 正斜杠 （/），以分号 （;），较低-号 (\<)，和更高版本-号 (>)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-542">An EDIFACT syntax that allows the following characters only: uppercase letters, all digits, blank, exclamation mark (!), quotation mark ("), percentage sign (%), ampersand (&), opening and closing parentheses ( "(" and ")"), asterisk (*), comma, dash (-), decimal point (.), forward slash (/), semicolon (;), less-than sign (\<), and greater-than sign (>).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-543">EDIFACT UNOB 语法 (EDIFACT UNOB syntax)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-543">EDIFACT UNOB syntax</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-544">允许以下 EDIFACT 语法仅字符： 大写和小写字母、 所有数字为空，感叹号 （！）、 引号 （"）、 百分比符号 （%）、 与号 (&)，单个引号 （'）、 左、 右括号 （"（"和")")，星号 （*），加号 （+），逗号，短划线 （-），小数点 （.）、 转发斜杠 （/）、 冒号 （:）、 分号 （;），较低-号 (\<)，等号 （=），更高的比号 (>) 和问号 （？）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-544">An EDIFACT syntax that allows the following characters only: lowercase and uppercase letters, all digits, blank, exclamation mark (!), quotation mark ("), percentage sign (%), ampersand (&), single quotation mark ('), opening and closing parentheses ( "(" and ")"), asterisk (*), plus sign (+), comma, dash (-), decimal point (.), forward slash (/), colon (:), semicolon (;), less-than sign (\<), equal sign (=), greater-than sign (>), and question mark (?).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-545">EIF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-545">EIF</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-546">请参阅“引擎输入文件 (EIF)”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-546">See Engine Input File (EIF).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-547">EIP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-547">EIP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-548">请参阅“企业集成平台 (EIP)”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-548">See Enterprise Integration Platform (EIP).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-549">电子数据交换 (electronic data interchange, EDI)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-549">electronic data interchange (EDI)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-550">两个计算机应用程序之间采用电子形式交换结构化和标准化文档的过程，在此过程中使用一组标准来控制计算机之间的文档（如采购订单和发票）传输。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-550">The electronic exchange of structured and normalized documents between two computer applications, using a set of standards to control the transfer of documents, such as purchase orders and invoices, between computers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-551">用于管理、商务和贸易的电子数据交换 (Electronic Data Interchange for Administration, Commerce and Trade, EDIFACT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-551">Electronic Data Interchange for Administration, Commerce and Trade (EDIFACT)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-552">一种全球通用的电子数据交换 (EDI)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-552">A worldwide electronic data interchange (EDI)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-553">element</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-553">element</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-554">在 EDI 中，指的是文档中级别最低的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-554">In EDI, the lowest level of information in a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-555">如发票号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-555">For example, invoice number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-556">在 XML 中，指的是以分层形式来组织信息的 XML 构造，即将一些元素嵌套在其他元素内，从而可形成深度不受限制的嵌套。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-556">In XML, an XML construct used to organize information in a hierarchical manner by nesting some elements within other elements to a potentially unlimited depth.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-557">元素组 (element groups)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-557">element groups</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-558">按照以下不同约束对 XML 结构中的同级元素进行分组：有顺序的序列（顺序组）、无顺序的序列（全部组）和多选一序列（选择组）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-558">Groupings of sibling elements in an XML structure according to different constraints: ordered sequence (Sequence Group), unordered sequence (All Group), and one-of-many (Choice Group).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-559">编码的协议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-559">encoding agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-560">两个贸易合作伙伴的业务配置文件之间的协议，可在交换消息时使用特定的编码协议（X12 或 EDIFACT）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-560">An agreement between the business profiles of two trading partners to use a specific encoding protocol (X12 or EDIFACT) while exchanging messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-561">编码协议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-561">encoding protocol</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-562">一种协议，它控制了业务到业务消息的结构与内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-562">A protocol that governs the structure and content of a business-to-business message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-563">业务配置文件的编码协议设置可定义业务部门用来发送和接收业务到业务消息的编码协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-563">The encoding protocol settings for a business profile define the encoding protocol that a business division uses to send and receive business-to-business messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-564">例如 X12、EDIFACT、HIPAA 和 EANCOM 都是编码协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-564">Some examples of encoding protocols are X12, EDIFACT, HIPAA, and EANCOM.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-565">加密密钥 (encryption key)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-565">encryption key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-566">用于加密或解密凭据信息的字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-566">A string used to encrypt or decrypt credentials information.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-567">结束类型更改请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-567">end type change request</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-568">使用管理控制台或 BTSTask 导入 BizTalk 应用程序 MSI 文件期间，项目类型部署到目标计算机的最后阶段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-568">The last stage of the deployment of an artifact type onto the destination computer, during an import of a BizTalk application MSI file using the Administration console or BTSTask.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-569">也称为项目类型的提交更改请求或提交导入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-569">Also known as a commit change request, or commit import for a type of artifact.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-570">端点</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-570">endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-571">位置的逻辑表示，通常采用 URL 形式，提供了已接收或已发送数据的物理地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-571">The logical representation of a location, typically expressed in URL form, providing a physical address for data received or sent.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-572">引擎输入文件 (Engine Input File, EIF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-572">Engine Input File (EIF)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-573">文档架构的已编译版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-573">A compiled version of a document schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-574">使用 EIF 可加速转换以在闭合用户组的其他用户中进行分发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-574">The EIF is used to expedite translations for distribution among other users in a closed user group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-575">只要使用 BizTalk Server 生成或编辑 XML 架构定义语言 (XSD) 架构，就会自动编译出 EIF。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-575">The EIF is automatically compiled whenever an XML Schema Definition language (XSD) schema is generated or edited, using BizTalk Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-576">登记 (enlist)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-576">enlist</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-577">将业务流程与要运行它的物理环境相关联的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-577">The process of associating an orchestration with the physical environment in which it will run.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-578">此过程包括指定将消息传入和传出业务流程所需的适配器，指定作为业务流程宿主的应用程序进程，以及创建路由指定的 MessageBox 订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-578">This includes specifying  the adapters needed to transport messages to and from the orchestration, the application process in which the orchestration is hosted, and creating the MessageBox subscriptions indicated by the routing.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-579">企业应用程序集成 (enterprise application integration)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-579">enterprise application integration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-580">将两个企业应用程序的数据或功能集成在一起的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-580">The process of bringing data or a function from an enterprise application together with that of another application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-581">企业集成平台 (EIP) (Enterprise Integration Platform, EIP)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-581">Enterprise Integration Platform (EIP)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-582">企业应用程序进行集成的环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-582">The environment in which enterprise application integration occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-583">此方案实际上是组合为一个方案的一组方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-583">This scenario is actually a class of scenarios grouped together as a single scenario.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-584">企业单一登录系统 (Enterprise Single Sign-On system)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-584">Enterprise Single Sign-On system</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-585">由 SSO 数据库、主密钥服务器以及一个或多个企业单一登录 (SSO) 服务器组成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-585">An SSO database, a master secret server, and one or more Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-586">这些服务器在 Windows 凭据和非 Windows 凭据之间建立映射，在 SSO 数据库中查找凭据并管理 SSO 系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-586">These servers do the mapping between the Windows and non-Windows credentials, look up the credentials in the SSO database, and are used for administering the SSO system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-587">SSO 数据库还用作配置存储，以保存适配器的自定义配置数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-587">The SSO database is also used as a configuration store to hold custom configuration data for adapters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-588">信封 (envelope)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-588">envelope</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-589">指的是一组结构化信息，这些信息与实例消息封装在一起，通常用于描述送达和处理信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-589">A structured set of information that wraps and accompanies an instance message, often describing delivery and processing information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-590">信封可以嵌套。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-590">Envelopes can be nested.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-591">信封架构 (envelope schema)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-591">envelope schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-592">使用几个附加属性指定信封结构的架构类型，这些属性是信封所特有的，它们指定了诸如标识封装数据流中的信封内容等信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-592">A type of schema that specifies the structure of an envelope, using several extra properties that are specific to envelopes and which specify information such as identifying the envelope contents in an enveloped data stream.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-593">执行循环 (execution cycle)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-593">execution cycle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-594">指在业务规则引擎内断言事实、计算条件的结果并执行操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-594">The assertion of facts, evaluation of conditions, and execution of actions within the Business Rule Engine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-595">执行模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-595">Execution Mode</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-596">确定阶段中管道组件执行模式的管道阶段属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-596">A pipeline stage property that determines the execution pattern of pipeline components in a stage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-597">执行模式可以设置为“全部”或“第一个匹配”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-597">The Execution Mode can be set to All or First Match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-598">在“全部”模式下，将按配置好的顺序执行阶段内的所有组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-598">In All mode, all the components within the stage are carried out in the configured sequence.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-599">当需要由多个组件完成一项特定的逻辑任务，并且需要执行所有这些组件时，可采用此模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-599">This mode is used when several components are required to complete a certain logical task, and they must all be executed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-600">在该管道阶段处理消息过程中，如果任意组件遇到错误，都会导致运行时错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-600">If any component encounters an error while processing a message that is going through this pipeline stage, a run-time error results.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-601">导出向导 (Export Wizard)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-601">Export Wizard</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-602">在 BizTalk 管理控制台启动的从 BizTalk 应用程序生成 MSI 文件的向导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-602">A wizard that you start from the BizTalk Administration Console to generate an MSI file from a BizTalk application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-603">之后你可以将此 MSI 文件复制到其他 BizTalk Server 实例，并使用“导入向导”导入 MSI 文件的资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-603">You can then copy this MSI file to a different instance of BizTalk Server and use the Import Wizard to import the resources of the MSI file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-604">快递 (express delivery)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-604">express delivery</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-605">表示传入消息和传出消息的持久性（存储在 SQL 数据库中）的消息传递类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-605">A type of message delivery that implies persistency (store in the SQL database), both for incoming messages and outgoing messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-606">可扩展样式表语言转换 (XSLT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-606">Extensible Stylesheet Language Transformations (XSLT)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-607">从早期的可扩展样式表语言 (XSL) 标准发展而来。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-607">Evolved from the early Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL) standard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-608">XSL 指定了 XML 数据表示和数据转换的语言定义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-608">XSL specifies a language definition for XML data presentation and data transformations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-609">数据表示是以某种格式和/或介质显示数据，数据有一定的样式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-609">Data presentation means displaying data in some format and/or medium, and concerns style.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-610">数据转换是将输入 XML 文档解析为节点树，然后将源树转换为结果树。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-610">Data transformation refers to parsing an input XML document into a tree of nodes, and then converting the source tree into a result tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-611">转换与数据交换有关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-611">Transformation concerns data exchange.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-612">外部消息格式 (external message format)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-612">external message format</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-613">消息在经 BizTalk Server 处理之前或之后的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-613">The format of the message before or after it is processed by BizTalk Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-614">有时也会使用术语“有线”(wire) 格式来指代外部消息格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-614">Sometimes the term "wire" format is also used when referring to external message format.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="f"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-615">F</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-615">F</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-616">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-616">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-617">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-617">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-618">方面 (facet)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-618">facet</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-619">一种 XML 架构定义语言 (XSD) 概念，用于限制元素或属性的取值范围，并为架构的实例提供验证参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-619">An XML Schema Definition language (XSD) concept for restricting the possible values that an element or attribute can take, providing validation parameters for instances of a schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-620">例如，可以为字符串数据指定最小长度和最大长度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-620">For example, a minimum and maximum length can be specified for string data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-621">不同类型的 facet 适用于不同类型的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-621">Different types of facets apply to different types of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-622">事实 (fact)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-622">fact</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-623">应用规则条件的用户数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-623">User data to which rule conditions are applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-624">在设计时，事实是指对该数据的引用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-624">At design time a fact is a reference to that data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-625">事实库 (fact base)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-625">fact base</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-626">计算规则条件的值时所依据的事实集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-626">A collection of facts against which rule conditions are evaluated.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-627">事实检索器（规则引擎）(fact retriever (Rule Engine))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-627">fact retriever (Rule Engine)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-628">一种用户定义的可选插件组件，用于实现 IFactRetriever 接口，以便收集业务策略所使用的长期事实。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-628">An optional, user-defined plug-in component that implements an IFactRetriever interface so that it can gather long-term facts for use by business policies.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-629">事实存储 (fact store)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-629">fact store</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-630">存储有关参与者的信息（包括角色和属性）的数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-630">The database that stores information, including role and attributes, about actors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-631">事实存储还提供分层浏览功能，以便操作可以确定参与者在组织内的相对位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-631">The fact store also provides hierarchy navigation so that actions can determine the relative positions of actors within an organization.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-632">事实存储管理器 (fact store manager)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-632">fact store manager</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-633">从各种事实检索器对象检索事实信息的组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-633">The component that retrieves the fact information from the various FactRetriever objects.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-634">故障转移传输 (failover transport)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-634">failover transport</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-635">一种辅助传输。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-635">A secondary transport.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-636">备选贸易合作伙伴协议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-636">fallback trading partner agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-637">在不存在显式协议时，BizTalk Server 用于业务到业务消息处理的一组设置集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-637">A collection of settings that BizTalk Server uses for business-to-business message handling, when no explicit agreement is present.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-638">文件适配器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-638">File adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-639">可以从文件系统读取消息并将消息提交给服务器的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-639">An adapter that can read messages from the file system and submits them to the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-640">文件适配器还可将服务器的消息写入文件系统中的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-640">The file adapter also writes messages from the server to a file on the file system.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-641">筛选器表达式属性 (Filter Expression property)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-641">Filter Expression property</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-642">接收形状中用于确定接收哪些消息的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-642">A property of a Receive shape that determines which messages can be received.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-643">接收形状要使用筛选器表达式，必须将激活属性设置为“True”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-643">The Receive shape must have the Activate property set to True to have a filter expression.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-644">查找消息视图 (Find Message view)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-644">Find Message view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-645">使用户可根据跟踪的消息属性查找消息的报表视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-645">A reporting view that enables users to find messages based on tracked message properties.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-646">FTP 适配器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-646">FTP adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-647">支持在 BizTalk Server 和 FTP 服务器之间交换文件的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-647">An adapter that enables exchange of files between BizTalk Server and FTP servers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-648">函数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-648">function</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-649">用于访问操作定义和谓词定义中的类成员的抽象表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-649">An abstraction that is used to access class members in both the action and predicate definitions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-650">函数用于操作中，在谓词中，函数被当作术语使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-650">A function is used in actions and as a term in a predicate.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-651">functoid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-651">functoid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-652">执行特定计算或数据处理的可执行模块，在构造 BizTalk Server 映射时可以图形方式使用该模块，从而提供比 XSLT 自身提供的转换还要丰富的转换基准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-652">An executable module that performs a specific calculation or data manipulation, and that is used graphically when constructing BizTalk Server maps to provide the basis for richer transformations than what is provided by XSLT on its own.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-653">Functoid IntelliSense</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-653">Functoid IntelliSense</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-654">当 functoid 配置中存在错误时，BizTalk 映射器功能可在网格图画上提高视觉提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-654">A BizTalk Mapper functionality in which visual cues are provided on the grid surface, when there are errors in functoid configuration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-655">functoid 工具箱 (functoid toolbox)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-655">functoid toolbox</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-656">Visual Studio 中充当 functoid 控件面板的可停靠窗口，可在构造映射过程中使用该窗口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-656">A dockable window in Visual Studio that serves as the palette of functoids available for use during map construction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-657">根据 functoid 的不同用途，它们被组织到不同的工具箱标签中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-657">Functoids are organized into different toolbox tabs based on their intended purpose.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-659">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-659">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-660">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-660">Definition</span></span>|

## <a name="h"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-677">H</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-677">H</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-678">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-678">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-679">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-679">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-680">处理程序 (handler)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-680">handler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-681">运行适配器的 BizTalk 主机实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-681">An instance of a BizTalk host on which an adapter is running.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-682">密切相关的文章</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-682">hash</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-683">通过将单向数学函数（有时也称为哈希算法）应用到任意数量的数据所获得的固定大小的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-683">A fixed-size result that is obtained by applying a one-way mathematical function (sometimes called a hash algorithm) to an arbitrary amount of data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-684">如果输入数据更改，则哈希值也随之更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-684">If the input data changes, the hash changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-685">哈希可用于许多操作，包括身份验证和数字签名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-685">The hash can be used in many operations, including authentication and digital signing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-686">也称为消息摘要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-686">Also known as message digest.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-687">运行状况监视</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-687">health monitoring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-688">为预先发现问题或解决问题而监视用于实施 BizTalk Server 解决方案的应用程序、组件和服务器的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-688">The process of monitoring applications, components, and servers on which a BizTalk Server solution is implemented for the purposes of preempting or fixing problems.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-689">运行状况监视多维数据集 (Health Monitoring cube)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-689">Health Monitoring cube</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-690">一种包含有关消息和服务的信息的联机分析处理 (OLAP) 多维数据集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-690">An online analytical processing (OLAP) cube that contain information about messages and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-691">BizTalk Server 中包含两个多维数据集：消息事实多维数据集和服务事实多维数据集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-691">Two cubes included with BizTalk Server are: Message Facts and Service Facts.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-692">分层视图 (hierarchical view)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-692">hierarchical view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-693">跟踪配置文件编辑器 (TPE) 的左窗格以及创建报表命名空间和业务活动视图的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-693">The left pane of the Tracking Profile Editor (TPE) and the area where the reporting namespaces and Business Activity views are created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-694">该视图主要用于表示跟踪配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-694">Its main purpose is to represent the tracking profile.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-695">历史记录数据库 (History database)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-695">History database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-696">特定于业务流程管理方案的后端数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-696">A backend database specific to the Business Process Management scenario.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-697">主机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-697">host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-698">代表一个或多个 BizTalk Server 运行时实例的逻辑容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-698">A logical container representing one or more BizTalk Server run-time instances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-699">这是一个包含有关驻留在其中的项目（即驻留在主机内的所有业务流程、架构、接收位置和适配器）的信息的进程空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-699">This is the process space within which information about artifacts resides (that is, all the orchestrations, schemas, receive locations, and adapters that reside within a host).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-700">主机还可充当 Windows 内的安全域 - 它代表一个虚拟进程边界，在该边界内主机实例在一个或多个服务器上运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-700">The host also serves as a security domain within Windows - it represents a virtual process boundary within which host instances run on one or more servers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-701">主机实例 (host instance)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-701">host instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-702">一种 Windows NT 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-702">A Windows NT Service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-703">主机实例是特定服务器上的主机的物理表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-703">A host instance is the physical representation of a host on a specific server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-704">主机实例级别设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-704">host instance–level setting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-705">一个 BizTalk 管理员可在 BizTalk 设置仪表板中修改的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-705">One of the settings that BizTalk administrators can modify in the BizTalk Settings Dashboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-706">示例包括与业务流程内存阻止相关的 .NET CLR 设置和属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-706">Examples include .NET CLR settings and properties related to an orchestration memory throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-707">特定于一个给定主机实例，主机级别设置实质上控制着对计算机资源（如 RAM 或 I/O）的使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-707">Specific to a given host instance, host-level settings essentially govern the use of a computer's resources (such as RAM or I/O).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-708">一个示例是最大值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-708">An example is Max.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-709">I/O 线程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-709">I/O Threads.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-710">主机级别设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-710">host-level setting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-711">一个 BizTalk 管理员可在 BizTalk 设置仪表板中修改的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-711">One of the settings that BizTalk administrators can modify in the BizTalk Settings Dashboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-712">示例包括：主机跟踪，以及与基于资源的阻止、基于速率的阻止和业务流程阻止相关的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-712">Examples include host tracking, and properties related to resource-based throttling, rate-based throttling, and orchestration throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-713">主机级别设置可将所有主机实例调整为按给定部署方式行动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-713">Host-level settings tweak the way all instances of host behave in a given deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-714">例如，如果对于 Host1 设置最大值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-714">For example, if for Host1 the setting Max.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-715">引擎线程更改为 200，Host1 的所有实例将都使用最多 200 个引擎线程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-715">engine threads is changed to 200, all instances of Host1 will work with a maximum of 200 engine threads.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-716">主机负载平衡</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-716">host load balancing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-717">将运行 BizTalk Server 的多个服务器添加到 BizTalk 组，然后配置进程内主机的多个实例以在这些服务器上运行的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-717">The process of adding multiple servers running BizTalk Server to a BizTalk group and then configuring multiple instances of an in-process host to run on these servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-718">这可以跨主机的多个实例分发在该主机中配置的服务和项目的执行，这可增强其可用性与可伸缩性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-718">This distributes the execution of services and artifacts configured in that host across multiple instances of the host, which enhances its availability and scalability.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-719">主机类型 (host type)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-719">host type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-720">确定主机在是 BizTalk Server 进程内还是进程外控制的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-720">A property that determines whether the host is controlled within or outside of the BizTalk Server process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-721">主机类型分为进程内和独立两种。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-721">Host types are In-process or Isolated.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-722">HTTP 适配器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-722">HTTP adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-723">支持在 BizTalk Server 和任何使用 HTTP 或 HTTPS 协议的应用程序之间交换消息的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-723">An adapter that enables exchange of messages between BizTalk Server and any application using the HTTP or HTTPS protocol.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="i"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-724">I</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-724">I</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-725">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-725">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-726">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-726">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-727">IDE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-727">IDE</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-728">请参阅“集成开发环境”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-728">See Integrated Development Environment.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-729">导入/导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-729">Import/export</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-730">在 BizTalk 设置仪表板中，导入/导出设置和绑定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-730">In BizTalk Settings Dashboard, to import/export settings and bindings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-731">将组、主机和主机实例的当前 BizTalk 设置导出并另存为 XML 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-731">The current BizTalk settings for group, host, and host instance are exported and saved as an XML file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-732">BizTalk 管理员导入这些设置，以将它们应用于另一个 BizTalk 环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-732">BizTalk administrators import these settings to apply them to another BizTalk environment.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-733">导入向导 (Import Wizard)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-733">Import Wizard</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-734">从 BizTalk 管理控制台启动的、将 MSI 文件中的资源导入 BizTalk 应用程序的向导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-734">A wizard that you start from the BizTalk Administration Console to import resources from an MSI file into a BizTalk application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-735">如果指定的应用程序不存在，则“导入向导”将自动创建该程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-735">If the specified application does not exist, the Import Wizard automatically creates it.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-736">独立组合 (independent composition)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-736">independent composition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-737">由两个操作组成的序列，其中第二个操作在开始处理业务逻辑之前并不依赖第一个操作的同步消息；第二个操作可以立即开始处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-737">The sequencing of two actions where the second action does not depend on a sync message from the first action before the second action begins processing business logic; the second action can begin immediately.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-738">infotip</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-738">infotip</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-739">一种工具提示，用于在 Web 视图和 Windows 资源管理器注释列（在使用详细信息视图时）中提供对桌面、窗口和开始菜单命令的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-739">A tooltip used to provide a description for desktop, window, and Start menu commands, in Web views, and in the Windows Explorer Comment column when Details view is used.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-740">继承性 (inheriting)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-740">inheriting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-741">贸易合作伙伴管理 (TPM) Web Services 中成员配置文件将继承其父组的所有首选项的概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-741">In the Trading Partner Management (TPM) Web service, the concept that a member profile will inherit all the preferences of its parent group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-742">如果是非继承组，则成员配置文件不继承父组的任何首选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-742">In the case of a non-inheriting group, the member profile does not inherit any preferences from the parent group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-743">非继承组可以改为继承组，但继承组不能改为非继承组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-743">A non-inheriting group can be changed to an inheriting group; however, an inheriting group cannot be changed to non-inheriting group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-744">可中断的业务流程 (interruptible orchestration)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-744">initerruptible orchestration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-745">运行中可在定义好的点中断的业务流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-745">An orchestration that can be interrupted in mid-process at well-defined points.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-746">进程内主机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-746">In-process host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-747">一种在 BizTalk Server 进程空间内运行的主机类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-747">A host type that operates within the BizTalk Server process space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-748">任何业务流程都可以登记到进程内主机上，任何发送处理程序都能以进程内主机为宿主。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-748">Any orchestration can be enlisted to an In-process host, and any send handler can be hosted by it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-749">进程内主机只能作为进程内主机的接收处理程序（文件适配器）的宿主。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-749">In-process hosts can only host receive handlers for In-process hosts (File adapter).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-750">进程内接收适配器 (In-process receive adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-750">In-process receive adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-751">驻留在 BizTalk Server 进程内的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-751">An adapter that is hosted in the BizTalk Server processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-752">该适配器由服务器进程进行创建、控制和毁坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-752">It is created, controlled, and destroyed by server processes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-753">安装向导</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-753">Installation Wizard</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-754">在“导入向导”的最后一步启动的将 BizTalk 应用程序安装到本地计算机上的向导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-754">A wizard that you can start during the final step of the Import Wizard to install a BizTalk application on the local computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-755">实例活动 (instance activity)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-755">instance activity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-756">处理一条或多条消息的一系列连续步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-756">A series of contiguous processing steps through which one or more messages flow.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-757">实例消息 (instance message)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-757">instance message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-758">BizTalk Server 处理的一组不连续运行时数据，通常表示特定的业务文档（如采购订单），它与定义其结构的 BizTalk Server 架构并不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-758">A discrete unit of run-time data flowing through BizTalk Server, usually representing a particular business document such as a purchase order, and as differentiated from the BizTalk Server schema that defines its structure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-759">集成开发环境 (Integrated Development Environment, IDE)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-759">Integrated Development Environment (IDE)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-760">一系列基于 Microsoft Windows 的用户界面 (UI) 工具，用于生成、测试和优化平台及其功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-760">A combined set of Microsoft Windows-based user interface (UI) tools for building, testing, and refining a platform and its features.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-761">侦听器 (interceptor)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-761">interceptor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-762">用于从正在处理的数据流中提取数据并将数据保存到存储的机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-762">A mechanism used to extract data from processing streams and persist the data to storage.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-763">交换 (interchange)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-763">interchange</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-764">EDI 中文档的逻辑组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-764">In EDI, a logical combination of documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-765">交换的目标接收方只能有一个。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-765">Interchanges are destined for a single recipient.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-766">在 BizTalk 消息传送中，交换是接收管道的拆装阶段或发送管道的组装阶段处理的数据正文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-766">In BizTalk messaging, an interchange is a body of data that is processed by the disassembly stage of a receive pipeline or the assembly stage of a send pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-767">交换包含零条或多条消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-767">The interchange contains zero or more messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-768">在接收管道中，拆装器从接收到的交换中提取消息，并沿接收管道向下继续传播这些消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-768">In a receive pipeline, the disassembler extracts the messages contained in the interchange it received, and propagates these messages further down the receive pipeline.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-769">交换头部 (interchange header)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-769">interchange header</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-770">EDI 中指示交换开始的交换部分或一组逻辑关联的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-770">In EDI, a part of an interchange, or group of logically associated documents, used to indicate the start of the interchange.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-771">交换尾部 (interchange trailer)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-771">interchange trailer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-772">EDI 中指示交换结束的交换部分或一组逻辑关联的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-772">In EDI, a part of an interchange, or group of logically associated documents, used to indicate the end of the interchange.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-773">组间适配器 (intergroup adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-773">intergroup adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-774">以两个 BizTalk Server 组之间的 Intranet/LAN 通信为目标而不需要中间存储的 BizTalk Server 适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-774">A BizTalk Server adapter that targets intranet/LAN communication between two BizTalk Server groups without requiring intermediate storage.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-775">内部消息格式 (internal message format)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-775">internal message format</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-776">由 BizTalk Server 处理消息之后或之前它的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-776">The format of the message after or before it is processed by BizTalk Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-777">例如，BizTalk Server 在接收管道开始处接收消息，其格式为外部格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-777">For example, BizTalk Server receives a message, at the start of the receive pipeline, in the external format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-778">当消息经过管道后，其格式就变为内部格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-778">After the message goes through the pipeline, it is in the internal format.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-779">独立主机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-779">Isolated host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-780">一种在 BizTalk Server 系统外部操作的主机类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-780">A host type that operates outside of the BizTalk Server installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-781">独立主机不支持业务流程登记、不能作为发送处理程序的宿主、不能使用主机跟踪功能，也不能作为组的默认主机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-781">An Isolated host cannot have orchestrations enlisted to it, host a send handler, use host tracking, or be used as the default host for the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-782">只有那些独立主机的接收处理程序（HTTP、SOAP）能以独立主机为宿主。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-782">Only those receive handlers for Isolated hosts (HTTP, SOAP) can be hosted by an Isolated host.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-783">独立的接收适配器 (isolated receive adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-783">isolated receive adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-784">驻留在非 BizTalk Server 进程中的接收适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-784">The receive adapter that is hosted in a process other than a BizTalk Server process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-785">该适配器由外部进程创建和控制，它在运行时向 BizTalk Server 进行注册以提交消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-785">This adapter is created and controlled by external process and it registers with BizTalk server at run time to submit messages.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="k"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-786">K</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-786">K</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-787">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-787">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-788">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-788">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-789">关键绩效指标 (KPI)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-789">Key Performance Indicator (KPI)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-790">由 Analysis Service 提供的可自定义的业务度量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-790">Customizable business metrics provided by Analysis Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-791">KPI 由用于生成行业标准目标和基准的相关属性和关联计算组成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-791">KPIs consist of relevant attributes and associated calculations that generate industry-standard goals and benchmarks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-792">KPI 集合包括度量值、目标、显示属性和差异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-792">A KPI collection includes a measure, a goal, display properties, and variances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-793">公司可以使用 KPI 来跟踪绩效并提高决策能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-793">Companies use KPIs to track performance and improve decision-making abilities.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="l"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-794">L</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-794">L</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-795">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-795">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-796">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-796">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-797">后期绑定端口 (late bound port)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-797">late bound port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-798">业务流程中定义的将“绑定”属性设置为“以后指定”的端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-798">A port defined in the orchestration, which has the Binding property set to Specify later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-799">后期绑定端口在绑定到物理端口时进行配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-799">A late bound port is configured when it is bound to a physical port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-800">使用 BizTalk 管理控制台来执行绑定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-800">The binding is performed using the    BizTalk Administration Console.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-801">行业应用程序 (line-of-business application)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-801">line-of-business application</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-802">对于企业运营至关重要的应用程序，如工资单管理系统、资源规划应用程序、供应链管理应用程序和会计应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-802">An application that is vital to running enterprises, such as payroll, resource planning, supply chain management, and accounting.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-803">实时数据 (live data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-803">live data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-804">当前正由 BizTalk Server 处理的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-804">Data that is currently being processed by BizTalk Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-805">本地唯一标识符 (locally unique identifier, LUID)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-805">locally unique identifier (LUID)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-806">BizTalk 组中唯一标识项目的项目名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-806">A name for an artifact that identifies it uniquely in the BizTalk group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-807">根据项目的类型，构成 LUID 的元素可能不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-807">The elements comprising the LUID may vary, depending on the type of artifact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-808">例如，BizTalk 程序集的 LUID 包括它的名称、版本、区域性及公钥标记，如 Microsoft.BizTalk.Hws.HwsPromotedProperties, Version=3.0.1.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-808">For example, the LUID for a BizTalk assembly includes its name, version, culture, and public key token, such as Microsoft.BizTalk.Hws.HwsPromotedProperties, Version=3.0.1.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-809">长期事务 (long-running transaction)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-809">long-running transaction</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-810">作为一个单元进行处理的操作集合，通常用于以可预测的可靠方式维持相应的状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-810">A collection of actions treated as a unit, typically used to maintain an appropriate state in a robust and predictable fashion.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-811">这种事务的运行时间可能无限长，并可包含多个嵌套事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-811">The transaction can take place over an indefinite period of time and contain several nested transactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-812">循环记录 (looping record)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-812">looping record</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-813">一种可以在实例消息中多次出现的结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-813">A structure that can have more than one occurrence in an instance message.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="m"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-814">M</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-814">M</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-815">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-815">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-816">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-816">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-817">管理数据库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-817">Management database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-818">一种 Microsoft SQL Server 数据库，用于存储组织中各种资源的配置信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-818">A Microsoft SQL Server database that stores the configuration information for resources in an organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-819">每个组织都有一个管理数据库（有时称为配置数据库）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-819">There is one Management database (sometimes referred to as the configuration database) per organization.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-820">地图 (map)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-820">map</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-821">定义一种规范的记录和字段与另一种规范的记录和字段之间对应关系的 XML 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-821">An XML file that defines the correspondence between the records and fields in one specification and the records and fields in another specification.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-822">映射包含一个可扩展样式表语言 (XSL) 样式表，BizTalk Server 可使用该样式表执行该映射中所描述的转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-822">A map contains an Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL) stylesheet that is used by BizTalk Server to perform the transformation described in the map.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-823">映射器网格 (mapper grid)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-823">mapper grid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-824">BizTalk 映射器主窗口中源架构和目标架构之间的多层中间区域，其中定义了数据映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-824">The multi-layered middle area of the main BizTalk Mapper window, between the source and destination schemas, in which data mapping is defined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-825">映射器网格页 (mapper grid page)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-825">mapper grid page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-826">映射器网格中单独的一层，用于将相关数据映射组织起来，从而与其他数据映射分开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-826">A single layer in the mapper grid, used to organize related data mappings separate from other data mappings.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-827">主密钥 (master secret)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-827">master secret</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-828">当企业单一登录 (SSO) 管理员请求密钥时，由主密钥服务器生成的密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-828">A key generated by the master secret server when an Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) Administrator requests it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-829">该密钥作为本地安全机构 (LSA) 密钥存储在主密钥服务器的注册表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-829">This secret key is stored in the registry as a Local Security Authority (LSA) secret on the master secret server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-830">只有 SSO 管理员可以访问此密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-830">Only SSO Administrators can access this secret key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-831">主密钥服务器 (master secret server)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-831">master secret server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-832">在分布式企业单一登录 (SSO) 环境中，注册表中保存有主密钥的计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-832">In a distributed Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) environment, the one computer that holds the master secret key in the registry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-833">可以有许多（不同计算机上的）SSO 服务器访问这一个 SSO 数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-833">There can be many SSO servers (on different machines) accessing this single SSO database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-834">但只能将其中一个 SSO 服务器指定为主密钥服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-834">Only one of these SSO servers is designated to be the master secret server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-835">message</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-835">message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-836">一种通常在两个运行的业务流程或应用程序之间进行数据交换的数据电子实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-836">An electronic instance of data, as typically exchanged between two running business processes or applications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-837">消息正文部分 (message body part)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-837">message body part</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-838">BizTalk Server 消息的主要部分，它包含实际负载，并在多数情况下包含 XML blob。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-838">The main part of a BizTalk Server message, which contains the actual payload, and in most cases an XML blob.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-839">所有消息最多只能有一个正文部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-839">All messages must have at most one body part.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-840">从 BizTalk Server 消息正文部分对应的数据流中读取的数据通常用于升级消息上下文属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-840">Typically the data read from the stream corresponding to the BizTalk Server message body part is used for promoting message context properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-841">因此，基于升级的属性的路由、发布或订阅通常根据正文部分执行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-841">Hence the routing, publication, or subscription that is based on promoted properties is generally done based on the body part.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-842">消息上下文 (message context)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-842">message context</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-843">包含 BizTalk Server 处理文档时所使用的各种属性的容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-843">A container for various properties that are used by BizTalk Server when processing a document.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-844">消息上下文属性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-844">message context properties</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-845">与消息关联的一组属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-845">A set of properties associated with the message.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-846">消息详细信息视图 (Message Details view)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-846">Message Details view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-847">一种在组中心页上，列出 MessageBox 中某个给定消息的所有已知信息的详细视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-847">On the Group Hub page, a detailed view of all known information for a given message in the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-848">通过单击一个（共两个）操作视图的透视表字段列表中的快捷方式菜单可查看此视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-848">This view is available through the shortcut menu in the PivotTable field list in one of two Operations views.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-849">消息摘要 (message digest)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-849">message digest</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-850">请参阅“哈希”术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-850">See Other Term: hash</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-851">消息事实多维数据集 (Message Facts cube)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-851">Message Facts cube</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-852">一种收集有关消息和服务的信息的联机分析处理 (OLAP) 多维数据集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-852">An online analytical processing (OLAP) cube that aggregates information about messages and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-853">BizTalk Server 附带有两个多维数据集：消息事实多维数据集和服务事实多维数据集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-853">Two cubes included out of the box are: Message Facts and Service Facts.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-854">消息流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-854">message flow</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-855">处理一条或多条消息的一系列连续步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-855">A series of contiguous processing steps through which one or more messages flow.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-856">“消息流”视图 (Message Flow view)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-856">Message Flow view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-857">一种在组中心页上显示特定消息处理事件历史记录的视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-857">A view on the Group Hub page that displays a history of processing events for specific messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-858">消息头部 (message header)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-858">message header</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-859">EDI 中指示文档开始的消息部分，它是包含有关一个事务的信息的一系列逻辑组合段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-859">In EDI, a part of the message used to indicate the start of a document, which is a bundle of logically combined segments containing information about one transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-860">在 ANSI X.12 中，消息等同于事务集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-860">In ANSI X.12, a message is equivalent to a transaction set.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-861">消息实例 (message instance)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-861">message instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-862">BizTalk Server 正在处理或已经序列化到 MessageBox 或跟踪数据库中以进一步进行处理或跟踪的消息实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-862">An instance of a message that BizTalk Server is either processing or has serialized into the MessageBox or Tracking datastore for further processing or tracking, respectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-863">在 BizTalk Server 中，通常指对消息、消息的升级属性及消息正文的引用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-863">Within BizTalk Server, this is usually a reference to the message, the promoted properties of the message, and the message body.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-864">消息度量视图 (Message Metrics view)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-864">Message Metrics view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-865">查看消息度量联机分析处理 (OLAP) 多维数据集的透视表视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-865">The PivotTableview into a message metrics online analytical processing (OLAP) cube.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-866">消息尾部 (message trailer)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-866">message trailer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-867">EDI 中用于指示文档结束的消息部分，它是包含有关一个事务的信息的一系列逻辑组合段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-867">In EDI, a part of the message used to indicate the end of a document, which is a bundle of logically combined segments containing information about one transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-868">在 ANSI X.12 中，消息等同于事务集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-868">In ANSI X.12, a message is equivalent to a transaction set.</span></span>|
