|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-943">合作伙伴协议管理 (PAM)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-943">Partner Agreement Management (PAM)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-944">BizTalk Server 管理控制台“参与方”节点中的用户界面，可从中设置参与方属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-944">A user interface in the Parties node of the BizTalk Server Administration Console where you set party properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-945">可设置 EDI 文档交换、EDI 批处理和 AS2 文档传输所涉及参与方的处理属性，以及在某个参与方缺席的情况下使用的全局属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-945">You can set processing properties for parties engaging in EDI document exchange, EDI batching, AS2 document transport, and global properties to be used in the absence of a party.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-946">参与方 (party)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-946">party</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-947">位于 BizTalk Server 外部并与业务流程交互的所有实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-947">Each entity outside of BizTalk Server that interacts with an orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-948">与你的组织有关系的所有合作伙伴都可以视作参与方，你的组织可能有数千个合作伙伴。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-948">All of the partners your organization deals with are considered parties, and your organization may have several has several thousands partners.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-949">参与方登记 (party enlistment)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-949">party enlistment</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-950">将参与方与角色关联在一起的机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-950">The mechanism that ties a party to a role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-951">可以在角色中登记参与方，这样业务流程就可以与该参与方进行交互了。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-951">You can enlist a party in a role, and that enables the orchestration to interact with the party</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-952">直通 (pass-through)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-952">pass-through</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-953">BizTalk Server 端口的一种配置，在这种配置下，由于发送端口上只使用一个筛选器表达式，所以接收端口与发送端口直接连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-953">A configuration of BizTalk Server ports such that a receive port is directly connected to a send port by using only one filter expression on a send port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-954">筛选器表达式的格式为 BTS.ReceivePortName == "名称或接收端口"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-954">The filter expression should take the form BTS.ReceivePortName == "Name or receive port".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-955">在这种配置下，接收端口收到的任何消息都会被直接路由到发送端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-955">In this configuration, any message that is received by the receive port is directly routed to a send port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-956">传递执行 BizTalk 2004 年的含义是不同的 BizTalk Server 2000 或 2002年中传递执行的含义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-956">The meaning of pass-through execution in BizTalk 2004 is different from the meaning of pass-through execution in BizTalk Server 2000 or 2002.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-957">在 BizTalk Server 2004 传递执行消息仍在管道中处理，并可能在端口以及转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-957">In BizTalk Server 2004, the pass-through execution message is still processed in pipelines and may be transformed in ports as well.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-958">性能监视</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-958">performance monitoring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-959">监视消息进程/接收率、运行的业务流程数、高速缓存命中数、一段时间的内存使用率等情况的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-959">The process of watching the message process/receive rate, number of running orchestrations, number of cache hits, memory usage over time, and so on.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-960">性能处理规则 (performance processing rules)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-960">performance processing rules</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-961">控制进程性能计数器或功能类型计数器的规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-961">Rules that govern process performance or capacity type counters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-962">外围网络</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-962">perimeter network</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-963">置于 Intranet 和 Internet 之间的保护 Intranet 免受未经授权的 Internet 用户访问的设备和子网的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-963">A collection of devices and subnets placed between an intranet and the Internet to help protect the intranet from unauthorized Internet users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-964">也称为 DMZ、外围安全区域和屏蔽式子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-964">Also known as DMZ, demilitarized zone, and screened subnet.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-965">物理（早期）绑定 (physical (early) binding)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-965">physical (early) binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-966">包含在程序集中供部署进程用于创建发送端口和接收端口的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-966">Information that is carried in the assembly and used by the deployment process to create send and receive ports.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-967">管道 (pipeline)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-967">pipeline</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-968">定义一个或多个处理阶段并将这些阶段链接起来，然后按指定顺序运行这些阶段以完成特定任务的软件基础结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-968">A software infrastructure that defines and links one or more processing stages, running them in prescribed order to complete a specific task.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-969">管道将处理过程分为多个阶段，阶段是对一类工作的抽象描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-969">Pipelines divide processing into stages, abstractions that describe a category of work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-970">管道还确定了执行每类工作的顺序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-970">They also determine the sequence in which each category of work is performed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-971">管道组件 (pipeline component)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-971">pipeline component</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-972">一种可放入管道中的基于 COM 或 .NET 的组件，用于对经过管道的消息执行某种处理操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-972">A COM or .NET-based component that can be placed into a pipeline to perform some processing action on the messages going through that pipeline.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-973">管道设计器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-973">Pipeline Designer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-974">BizTalk Server 中用于创建和配置管道的图形用户界面工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-974">A graphical user-interface tool used to create and configure pipelines in BizTalk Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-975">策略 (policy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-975">policy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-976">版本化的业务规则集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-976">A versioned collection of business rules.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-977">端口连接线 (port connector line)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-977">port connector line</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-978">用于指示发送/接收形状和端口形状上的操作之间的连接的线条。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-978">A line showing the connection between a Send/Receive shape and an operation on a Port shape.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-979">端口连接线两端的终结点都必须连接到形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-979">Neither endpoint of a port connector line can remain unattached.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-980">端口类型 (port type)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-980">port type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-981">一种属性，用于定义一组已调用允许在终结点执行的操作的消息交互模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-981">A property that defines the set of message interaction patterns called operations that are permitted at that endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-982">操作可以是发送或接收一条消息的单向操作，也可以是发送（接收）消息之后再接收（发送）响应的请求-响应操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-982">An operation can be one-way, in which case one message is sent or received, or it could be request-response in which case a message is sent (or received) and a response is received (or sent).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-983">位置平面文件 (positional flat file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-983">positional flat file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-984">用于表示某种业务文档的一种文件格式类型，这种业务文档中的记录和字段的长度都固定不变，无需任何分隔符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-984">A type of file format used to represent business documents in which the records and fields have a fixed length, eliminating the need for delimiters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-985">专用队列 (private queue)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-985">private queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-986">未作为 Active Directory 对象发布的队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-986">A queue that is not published as an Active Directory object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-987">BizTalk 消息队列完全支持将消息发送或接收到专用队列中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-987">BizTalk message queuing fully supports the sending and receiving of messages into private queues.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-988">流程图面 (process surface)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-988">process surface</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-989">业务流程设计器中设计图面的中间区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-989">The middle area of the design surface in the Orchestration Designer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-990">该区域用于设计业务流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-990">This area is used to design orchestrations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-991">项目设计器 (Project Designer)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-991">Project Designer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-992">构成项目的服务、端口和绑定的可视化表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-992">A visual representation of the services, ports, and bindings that make up a project.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-993">用户可通过在项目设计器中添加和删除服务、创建和删除服务的兼容端口之间的绑定来编辑这些可视项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-993">Users can edit the visual items in the Project Designer by adding and removing services, and creating and removing bindings between compatible ports on the services in the designer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-994">属性升级</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-994">property promotion</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-995">通过该特定的消息属性写入到作为属性字段与消息关联的消息上下文的机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-995">The mechanism through which specific message properties are written to the message context associated with the message as property fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-996">写入到消息上下文属性字段被视为提升的属性的属性 ( **IsPromoted**的字段的属性设置为**True**)，并且需要一个关联的属性架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-996">Properties written to the message context as property fields are considered to be promoted properties (the **IsPromoted** property of the field is set to **True**) and require an associated property schema.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-997">BizTalk Server Messaging Engine 为了文档路由邮件跟踪，并用于在业务流程中的评估使用属性字段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-997">Property fields are used by the BizTalk Server Messaging Engine for purposes of document routing, message tracking, and for evaluation in orchestrations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-998">消息的消息上下文存储于 MessageBox 数据库的后台处理表中该消息对应行的 imgContext 列中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-998">The message context for a message is stored in the imgContext column of the row for the message in the spool table of the MessageBox database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-999">属性架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-999">property schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1000">与 BizTalk Server 架构关联的架构，用于将文档中要升级到消息上下文的元素字段标识为属性字段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1000">A schema that you associate with a BizTalk Server schema, and used to identify the element fields in a document that will be promoted to the message context as property fields.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1001">协议设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1001">protocol setting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1002">用于定义如何为特定的业务到业务协议而支持业务交易的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1002">A setting that defines how business transactions are to be supported for a specific business-to-business protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1003">针对每一个业务到业务协议（合作伙伴可通过此协议进行通信），每一个业务配置文件都定义了处理消息（编码）或传输消息（传输）的各种设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1003">Each business profile defines the various settings for processing messages (encoding) or transmitting messages (transport) for each of the business-to-business protocols over which the partner can communicate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1004">协议设置可以用于编码协议或传输协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1004">A protocol setting can be for encoding protocols or for a transport protocol.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1005">公共队列 (public queue)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1005">public queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1006">作为 Active Directory 对象发布的队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1006">A queue that is published as an Active Directory object.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1007">发布-订阅 (publication-subscription)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1007">publication-subscription</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1008">请参阅“发布/订阅结构”术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1008">See Other Term: publish/subscribe architecture</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1009">发布/订阅结构 (publish/subscribe architecture)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1009">publish/subscribe architecture</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1010">发布和订阅的组合，用于在子系统之间移动消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1010">The combination of publication and subscription used  to move messages between subsystems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1011">例如，接收端口接收消息，然后处理消息并发布到 MessageBox。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1011">For example, receive ports receive messages, process them and  publish them to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1012">BizTalk Server 将这些消息路由到订阅业务流程或发送端口，订阅业务流程或发送端口进一步处理这些文档，并将它们重新发布到 MessageBox 或发送到外部系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1012">BizTalk Server routes these messages to subscribing orchestrations or send ports that further process the documents and either republish them to the MessageBox or send them to external systems.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1013">发布</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1013">publishing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1014">将消息实例存储到 MessageBox 数据库中的操作，从而使消息实例与使用相应消息类型的应用程序的订阅相匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1014">The act of storing a message instance in the MessageBox database so that it can be matched to a subscription from a consuming application.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="q"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1015">Q</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1015">Q</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1016">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1016">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1017">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1017">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1018">查询表达式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1018">Query Expression</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1019">“组中心”页中可用于创建和运行针对 BizTalk 跟踪数据库的查询的一组查询子句。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1019">A group of query clauses on the Group Hub page that you can use to create and run queries against the BizTalk Tracking database.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="r"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1020">R</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1020">R</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1021">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1021">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1022">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1022">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1023">范围维度 (range dimension)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1023">range dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1024">在 BAM 中，用于创建条件范围的维度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1024">In BAM, a dimension used to create ranges of crirteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1025">例如，可以创建低 (0-100)、中 (100-500) 和高 (500-1000) 三个范围来描述销售量的数量级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1025">For example, you could create Low (0-100), Medium (100-500), and High (500-1000) ranges to describe sales of numerical units.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1026">回执生成器 (receipt generator)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1026">receipt generator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1027">生成一份假的回执以便从重试队列中删除消息的组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1027">A component that generates a fake receipt to remove a message from the Retry Queue.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1028">如果消息传送端口配置为使用可靠消息传送机制，则使用该组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1028">This component is used if a messaging port is configured to use Reliable Messaging.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1029">接收处理程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1029">receive handler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1030">运行接收适配器的 BizTalk 主机的实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1030">An instance of a BizTalk host on which a receive adapter is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1031">接收处理程序是监听程序组件、终结点管理器组件和 MessageAgent 组件的逻辑容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1031">A receive handler is a logical container for a Listener component, an Endpoint Manager component, and a MessageAgent component.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1032">接收处理程序主机类型 (receive handler host type)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1032">receive handler host type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1033">一种用于限制主机类型的属性，该主机可作为特定接收处理程序的宿主。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1033">A property that restricts the host type by which a particular receive handler can be hosted.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1034">接收位置 (receive location)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1034">receive location</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1035">位置（如 URL）和适配器类型的设计时物理概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1035">The physical, design-time notion of a location (such as a URL) and an adapter type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1036">BizTalk Server 管理控制台的主机节点中的接收位置定义了接收功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1036">A receive location in the Host node in the BizTalk Server Administration console defines the receive functionality.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1037">接收管道</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1037">receive pipeline</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1038">在适配器接收到消息后，但在将消息发布到 MessageBox 数据库之前对消息执行的管道过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1038">A pipeline that is executed on messages after they have been received by an adapter and before they are published into the MessageBox database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1039">接收端口 (receive port)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1039">receive port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1040">相似接收位置的逻辑分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1040">A logical grouping of similar receive locations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1041">重新部署 (redeploy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1041">redeploy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1042">重新部署目标环境中已存在的程序集是指删除旧的程序集并部署新的程序集的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1042">The act of redeploying an assembly that already exists in the target environment by deleting the old bits and deploying the new ones.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1043">解除冻结 (rehydrate)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1043">rehydrate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1044">在发生某种事件（如接收到消息）后，在内存中激活位于持久存储中的空闲业务流程的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1044">To activate an idle orchestration in memory from persistent storage as a result of some event taking place, such as a message being received.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1045">关联视图</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1045">Relevance view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1046">通过 BizTalk 映射器，架构元素的非关联同级元素会折叠，以提供更精简的架构视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1046">A view in BizTalk Mapper whereby non-relevant siblings of a schema element collapse to provide a more compact view of the schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1047">这会减少所需的滚动，而集中于架构和映射的有用部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1047">This reduces the need for scrolling, and brings the focus to the useful parts of the schema and map.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1048">报告视图 (Reporting views)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1048">Reporting vews</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1049">显示一个或多个业务流程的一组分层视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1049">A hierarchical set of views that show a business process or processes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1050">存储库 (repository)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1050">repository</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1051">用于存储 Analysis Service 使用的元数据的存储容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1051">The storage container for the metadata used by Analysis Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1052">元数据以表格形式存储在关系数据库中，用于定义分析服务器对象的参数和属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1052">Metadata is stored in tables in a relational database and is used to define the parameters and properties of Analysis server objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1053">当 BizTalk 浏览器以只读模式访问数据时，XML 工具以读取-写入模式使用库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1053">XML tools use the repository in read-write mode, while BizTalk Explorer accesses the data in read-only mode.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1054">请求-响应适配器 (request-response adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1054">request-response adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1055">接收客户端的请求消息，将消息提交给服务器，等待响应，然后将响应发送回客户端的接收适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1055">A receive adapter that receives a request message from the client, submits it to the server, waits for a response, and then sends the response back to the client.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1056">返回形状 (Return shape)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1056">Return shape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1057">在业务流程真正结束前用于在某点中止该业务流程的形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1057">A shape used to terminate an orchestration at some point before the orchestration's true end.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1058">以下是一个示例：如果通过安全检查，则继续，否则返回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1058">An example of this might be: If (security check passed) continue, else Return.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1059">角色 (role)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1059">role</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1060">使用服务或实现服务的端口类型集合，提供参与方与业务流程交互的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1060">A collection of port types that either uses a service or implements a service, providing the means by which parties interact with orchestration(s).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1061">例如，业务流程可能使用发运方角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1061">For example, an orchestration might use the role of a Shipper.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1062">该发运方将有一两个关联的参与方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1062">The Shipper would have one or two parties associated with it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1063">当业务流程确定使用哪家发运公司来发运货物时，它会比较发运方角色中各个参与方的价格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1063">When the orchestration decides which shipping company to use to ship an item, it compares the prices of the parties in the Shipper role.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1064">角色链接 (role link)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1064">role link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1065">指的是通过消息定义的角色和双向交互中使用的端口类型之间的关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1065">The relationship between roles by defined by the message and port types used in the interactions in both directions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1066">角色链接类型 (role link type)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1066">role link type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1067">用于确定两项服务或业务流程之间的关系的属性，它定义该关系中每项服务的职责并指定每个角色提供的端口类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1067">A property that characterizes the relationship between two services or orchestrations by defining the part played by each of the services in the relationship and specifying the port types provided by each role.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1068">根节点</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1068">root node</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1069">BizTalk Server 架构中代表该架构指定的业务文档中最顶端的 XML 元素的节点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1069">A node within a BizTalk Server schema that represents the outermost XML element in the business document specified by the schema.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1070">RTA 时段 (RTA window)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1070">RTA window</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1071">定义聚合实时聚合 (RTA) 中的数据的时间段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1071">Defines the time period over which the data in a real-time aggregation (RTA) is aggregated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1072">例如，如果该时间段为一天并且时间点为现在，则你只会看到最近 24 小时内的数据的聚合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1072">For example, if the time period is one day and the point in time is now, then you see aggregations only on the data from the last 24 hours.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1073">随着该时间点不断变化，RTA 时段中的时间段也在变化；因此，它也称作变化时间段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1073">As the point in time is continuously changing, the time period in the RTA window is also changing; therefore, it is also referred to as a moving time window.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1074">规则 (rule)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1074">rule</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1075">条件和操作对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1075">A pairing of conditions and actions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1076">规则集 (rule set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1076">rule set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1077">相似规则的逻辑分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1077">A logical grouping of similar rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1078">可将规则集看作规则引擎的一种分组/分区机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1078">This can be viewed as a grouping/partitioning mechanism of the rule engine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1079">规则引擎框架 (Rules Engine Framework)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1079">Rules Engine Framework</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1080">应用程序开发人员用来编写基于规则的应用程序时所使用的 .NET 组件库、API 和服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1080">The .NET component library, APIs, and services used by application developers to write rule-based applications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1081">规则引擎更新服务 (Rules Engine Update service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1081">Rules Engine Update service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1082">执行动态策略更新的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1082">A service that performs dynamic policy updates.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1083">规则存储 (Rules store)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1083">Rules store</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1084">持久存储策略的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1084">A location for persisting policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1085">SQL Server 数据库是默认的规则存储。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1085">A SQL Server database is the default rule store.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="s"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1086">S</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1086">S</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1087">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1087">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1088">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1088">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1089">架构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1089">schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1090">消息的结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1090">The structure for a message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1091">架构可以包含多个子架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1091">A schema can contain multiple sub-schema.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1092">架构编辑器扩展 (Schema Editor Extension)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1092">Schema Editor extension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1093">软件模块扩展 BizTalk 编辑器支持的基本 XML/XSD 功能时所使用的机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1093">The mechanism through which software modules extend the basic XML/XSD functionality supported by BizTalk Editor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1094">架构编辑器扩展通常为 BizTalk 架构中的一个或多个节点添加补充属性，以表示这些节点的特定语义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1094">Schema Editor Extensions typically add supplemental properties to one or more nodes in BizTalk schemas to represent their particular semantics.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1095">屏蔽式子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1095">screened subnet</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1096">请参阅“外围网络”术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1096">See Other Term: perimeter network</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1097">安全套接字层 (Secure Sockets Layer)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1097">Secure Sockets Layer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1098">一种协议，它通过使用数据加密、 数字证书和公钥加密的组合提高数据通信的安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1098">A protocol that improves the security of data communication by using a combination of data encryption, digital certificates, and public key cryptography.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1099">SSL 支持在网络中进行身份验证并增强数据安全性和隐私。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1099">SSL enables authentication and increases data integrity and privacy over networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1100">SSL 不提供授权或不可否认性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1100">SSL does not provide authorization or nonrepudiation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1101">段 (segment)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1101">segment</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1102">EDI 中元素的某种逻辑组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1102">In EDI, a logical combination of elements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1103">例如，名称和地址详细信息组合为一个段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1103">For example, name and address details are combined in one segment.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1104">段标记 (segment tag)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1104">segment tag</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1105">EDI 中段的唯一标识符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1105">In EDI, a unique identifier for a segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1106">例如，在 EDIFACT 内，段标记是置于文档内各个元素之前的三个大写字母代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1106">Within EDIFACT, for example, segment tags are three-letter uppercase codes that prefix the elements within a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1107">在 ANSI X.12 中，段标记是两个或三个大写字母代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1107">In ANSI X.12, the segment tags are two or three-letter uppercase codes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1108">段标记类似于记录类型标识符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1108">A segment tag is similar to a record type identifier.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1109">发送处理程序 (send handler)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1109">send handler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1110">与发送适配器关联的 BizTalk 主机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1110">A BizTalk host with which the send adapter is associated.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1111">发送管道</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1111">send pipeline</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1112">从 BizTalk Server 发送消息之前对该消息执行的管道过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1112">A pipeline that is executed on messages before they are sent out of the BizTalk server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1113">发送端口 (send port)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1113">send port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1114">指发送消息的目标位置或接收消息的目标位置，以及用来实现通信操作的技术。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1114">The location to which messages are sent or from which messages are received, and the technology that is used to implement the communication action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1115">该位置由端口名称唯一标识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1115">The location is uniquely identified by the name of the port.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1116">发送端口组 (send port group)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1116">send port group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1117">发送端口的逻辑分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1117">A logical grouping of send ports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1118">消息发送到发送端口组后，会被路由到所有相关的发送端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1118">When a message is sent to a send port group, it is routed to all of the associated send ports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1119">也称为分发列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1119">Also referred to as a distribution list.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1120">服务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1120">service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1121">即执行特定系统功能的程序、例程或进程，用于支持操作系统级别的其他程序（如 Windows NT 服务）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1121">A program, routine, or process that performs a specific system function to support other programs at the operating systems level, such as a Windows NT service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1122">服务指运行在服务器上的 Windows NT 服务或 COM+ 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1122">A service is a Windows NT service or a COM+ service that runs on a server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1123">服务实例 (service instance)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1123">service instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1124">通常是指，BizTalk Server 正在处理或已经序列化到 MessageBox 中以便进一步处理或跟踪的业务流程实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1124">Generally refers to an instance of an orchestration that BizTalk Server is either processing or has serialized into the MessageBox for further processing or tracking.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1125">这通常为业务流程状态的序列化表示形式，引用业务流程中使用的所有消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1125">This is usually a serialized representation of the state of the orchestration and references to any messages in use within the orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1126">在消息上下文中，一个服务实例应用于一个端口实例，例如一个接收端口，在该端口中，输入是接收位置，输出则发布到 MessageBox 数据库，或者一个发送端口，在该端口中，输入为 MessageBox ，输出则通常为一个发送适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1126">In the context of messaging, a service instance applies to an instance of a port, for example, a receive port where the input is the receive location and the output is publishing to the MessageBox database, or a send port where the input is the MessageBox and the output is typically a send adapter.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1127">服务度量视图 (Service Metrics view)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1127">Service Metrics view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1128">查看服务度量 OLAP 多维数据集的透视表视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1128">A PivotTable view into the service metrics OLAP cube.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1129">它以前是聚合视图的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1129">Formerly part of Aggregation view.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1130">会话</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1130">session</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1131">在两台主机之间创建的一种用于交换数据的逻辑连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1131">A logical connection created between two hosts to exchange data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1132">通常情况下，会话使用排序和确认方式发送数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1132">Typically, sessions use sequencing and acknowledgments to send data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1133">形状 (shape)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1133">shape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1134">业务流程中一个或一组操作的图形表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1134">A graphical representation of an action or grouping of actions in an orchestration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1135">形状连接线 (shape connector line)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1135">shape connector line</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1136">用于链接形状并确定形状在业务流程中的相对顺序的线条。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1136">A line used to link shapes and determine their relative order in an orchestration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1137">简单形状 (Simple shape)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1137">Simple shape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1138">业务流程中不能折叠也不能包含其他形状的形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1138">A shape in an orchestration that cannot be collapsed and cannot contain other shapes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1139">单一登录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1139">Single Sign-On</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1140">请参阅“企业单一登录系统”术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1140">See Other Term: Enterprise Single Sign-On system</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1141">单一登录管理 (Single Sign-On administration)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1141">Single Sign-On administration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1142">一种对象模型，通过管理命令行实用程序（如 ssomanage 和 ssoconfig）和 Windows 管理规范 (WMI) 以及 BizTalk 浏览器访问，用于配置存储方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1142">The object model accessed by administrative command line utilities (such as ssomanage and ssoconfig), and by Windows Management Instrumentation (WMI) and BizTalk Explorer for configuration store scenarios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1143">该组件通过 SSO 服务器与 SSO 数据库通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1143">This component communicates with the SSO database using the SSO Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1144">单一登录管理员组 (Single Sign-On Administrators group)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1144">Single Sign-On Administrators group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1145">具有最高级别授权的管理员，通常可设置密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1145">The Administrator who has the highest level of authority and typically sets up the encryption key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1146">单一登录关联应用程序管理员组 (Single Sign-On Affiliate Application Administrators group)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1146">Single Sign-On Affiliate Application Administrators group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1147">一种管理员，可以创建和管理关联应用程序、为每个关联应用程序指定单一登录应用程序管理员帐户，并可执行单一登录应用程序管理员和单一登录应用程序用户可以执行的所有管理任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1147">Administrators who can create and manage affiliate applications, specify the Single Sign-On Application Administrators account for each affiliate application, and perform all the administration tasks that the Single Sign-On Application Administrators and Single Sign-On application users can do.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1148">单一登录应用程序管理员组 (Single Sign-On Application Administrators group)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1148">Single Sign-On Application Administrators group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1149">专为每个关联应用程序指定的管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1149">Administrators who are assigned specifically to each affiliate application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1150">单一登录客户端实用程序 (Single Sign-On client utilities)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1150">Single Sign-On client utilities</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1151">作为部分管理功能供最终用户使用的实用程序，用于提供用户在 SSO 数据库中的凭据映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1151">Available as part of the Administration feature, utilities for end-users to provide their credential mappings in the SSO database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1152">SSO 服务器可使用这些实用程序来与 SSO 数据库通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1152">These are used by the SSO server to communicate with the SSO database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1153">企业单一登录 (SSO) 数据库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1153">Single Sign-On (SSO) database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1154">存储企业单一登录 (SSO) 凭据的数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1154">The database in which Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) credentials are stored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1155">其他数据库存储 URL 和发送端口；只有一个数据库具有密钥子服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1155">Other databases store the URLs and send ports; only one has the secret sub-service.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1156">单一登录服务器 (Single Sign-On server)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1156">Single Sign-On server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1157">安装了企业单一登录 (SSO) 服务的服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1157">The server on which the Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) service is installed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1158">单一登录服务 (Single Sign-On services)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1158">Single Sign-On services</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1159">通过访问 SSO 数据库中的凭据来支持适配器单一登录的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1159">Services that enable single sign-on for adapters by accessing credentials in the SSO database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1160">这些服务用来管理 SSO 数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1160">These services are used to manage and administer the SSO database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1161">作为配置存储，这些服务还用来访问适配器的配置数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1161">As a configuration store, these services are used to access configuration data for adapters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1162">智能标记 (Smart Tag)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1162">Smart Tag</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1163">一种图形警告，用于指明形状尚未配置完全并提供如何继续操作的提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1163">A graphical warning that a shape is not fully configured, and which provides hints on how to proceed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1164">SMTP 适配器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1164">SMTP adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1165">实现 SMTP 协议（即发送电子邮件）以便与行业应用程序交互的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1165">An adapter that implements the SMTP protocol (that is, sends e-mail messages) to interact with line-of-business applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1166">该适配器只包括发送处理程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1166">This adapter includes only the send handler.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1167">SOAP 适配器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1167">SOAP adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1168">实现 SOAP 协议以便与行业应用程序交互，将业务流程发布为 Web Services 并使用外部 Web Services 的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1168">An adapter that implements the SOAP protocol to interact with line-of-business applications, publishes orchestrations as Web services, and consumes external Web services.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1169">SOAP 错误 (SOAP fault)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1169">SOAP fault</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1170">由 Web Services 返回的、传达该 Web Services 中的应用程序异常的错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1170">An error message returned by a Web service that conveys an application exception in the Web service.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1171">SOAP 标头</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1171">SOAP header</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1172">SOAP 消息信封中包含的可选元素，包含与 XML Web Services 方法的主要功能不直接相关的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1172">An optional element contained within the envelope of a SOAP message that can contain data not dirrectly related to the XML Web service method's primary functionality.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1173">SOAP 消息 (SOAP message)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1173">SOAP message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1174">格式正确的 XML 文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1174">A well-formed XML document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1175">此消息应使用 SOAP 信封和 SOAP 编码命名空间，并且应包含可选的 XML 声明，声明后跟 SOAP 信封（根元素）。此消息由可选的 SOAP 标头和 SOAP 消息正文组成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1175">It should use the SOAP envelope and SOAP encoding namespaces and include an optional XML declaration, followed by a SOAP envelope (the root element), which is made up of an optional SOAP header and a SOAP message body.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1176">SOAP 消息跟踪 (SOAP message tracing)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1176">SOAP message tracing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1177">在已发布的 Web Services 中设置断点以将详细的异常信息返回到 Web 客户端的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1177">A method for setting a breakpoint in a published Web service to return detailed exceptions to a Web client.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1178">要求响应适配器 (solicit-response adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1178">solicit-response adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1179">一种双向发送适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1179">A two-way send adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1180">要求响应发送适配器将 BizTalk Server 的请求消息发送到目标，等待响应消息，然后将响应消息提交回 BizTalk Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1180">A solicit-response send adapter sends a request message from BizTalk Server to a destination, waits for a response message, and then submits the response message back to BizTalk Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1181">源架构 (source schema)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1181">source schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1182">BizTalk Server 映射中使用的代表输出实例消息结构的架构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1182">The schema used in a BizTalk Server map that represents the structure of the output instance messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1183">SQL 适配器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1183">SQL adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1184">在 BizTalk Server 和 SQL Server 数据库之间交换信息的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1184">An adapter that exchanges information between BizTalk Server and a SQL Server database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1185">SSO</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1185">SSO</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1186">请参阅“企业单一登录系统”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1186">See Enterprise Single Sign-On system.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1187">阶段 (stage)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1187">stage</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1188">专用于完成某类特定工作的那部分管道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1188">A portion of a pipeline dedicated to completing a certain category of work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1189">阶段中的管道组件用于完成实际的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1189">The pipeline components within the stage complete the actual tasks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1190">过渡数据库 (staging database)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1190">staging database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1191">测试人员用于将程序集及其绑定部署到测试数据库或过渡数据库的数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1191">A database used by a tester to deploy the assembly with its bindings to the test or staging database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1192">静态适配器 (static adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1192">static adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1193">使用适配器框架提供的用户界面的适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1193">An adapter that uses the user interface provided by the adapter framework.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1194">静态端口 (static port)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1194">static port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1195">具有关联的目标地址和适配器类型的发送端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1195">A send port that has a destination address and adapter type associated with it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1196">与动态发送端口相反，静态发送端口在运行时不能更改其配置，并始终用来向唯一一个目标地址发送消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1196">As opposed to a dynamic send port, a static send port cannot change its configuration at run time and is always used to send messages to only one destination address.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1197">强名称密钥文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1197">strong name key file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1198">包含项目的标识（即该项目的简单文本名称、版本号和区域性信息（如果提供））以及公钥和数字签名的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1198">A file that contains the identity for an assembly - its simple text name, version number, and culture information (if provided) - plus a public key and a digital signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1199">它是使用相应私钥从程序集文件生成的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1199">It is generated from an assembly file using the corresponding private key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1200">（程序集文件包含程序集清单，该清单中包含构成程序集的所有文件的名称和哈希值。）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1200">(The assembly file contains the assembly manifest, which contains the names and hashes of all the files that make up the assembly.)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1201">提交 (submit)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1201">submit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1202">指的是这样一种操作：将消息和关联属性放在 MessageBox 数据库的相应表中，然后扫描订阅目录，寻找谓词与该消息属性相符的订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1202">The act of placing a message and associated properties in the appropriate tables in the MessageBox database and scanning the Subscription directory for subscriptions whose predicates match the properties of the message.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1203">subscribe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1203">subscribe</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1204">一种 BizTalk 机制，指示 MessageBox 将属性符合指定参数的消息（订阅）路由到相应进程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1204">A BizTalk mechanism for instructing the MessageBox to route messages with properties that meet specified parameters (subscriptions) to the appropriate processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1205">例如，发送端口筛选器在 MessageBox 中创建订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1205">For example, send port filters create subscriptions in the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1206">当消息发布到符合筛选器规范的 MessageBox 时，BizTalk Server 会将消息路由到订阅发送端口进行处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1206">When messages are published to the MessageBox that match the filter specification, BizTalk Server routes the messages to the subscribing send port for processing.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1207">订阅 (subscription)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1207">subscription</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1208">将与指定属性比较标准相符的消息路由到工作队列中的机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1208">A mechanism to route messages that match certain property comparison criteria into a Work queue.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1209">订阅数据库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1209">Subscription database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1210">包含 MessageBox 组的所有订阅的 MessageBox 数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1210">The MessageBox database that contains all of the subscriptions for a MessageBox group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1211">挂起的实例 (suspended instance)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1211">suspended instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1212">由于系统或消息中出现错误，BizTalk Server 已停止处理的消息或业务流程实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1212">An instance of a message or orchestration that BizTalk Server has stopped processing, due to an error in the system or the message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1213">通常，根据系统问题的解决办法，由系统错误导致的挂起实例是可恢复的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1213">Generally, suspended instances caused by system errors are resumable upon resolution of the system issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1214">而由于消息问题导致的挂起实例通常不可恢复，且消息本身必须修复并重新提交到 BizTalk Server 系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1214">Often, suspended instances due to a message problem are not resumable, and the message itself must be fixed and resubmitted to the BizTalk Server system.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1215">挂起队列 (Suspended queue)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1215">Suspended queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1216">包含处理期间出现错误或故障的工作项的队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1216">A queue that contains work items for which an error or failure was encountered during processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1217">挂起队列将一直存储这些消息，直到它们被纠正、重新处理或被删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1217">A suspended queue stores the messages until they can be corrected and reprocessed, or deleted.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="t"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1218">T</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1218">T</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1219">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1219">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1220">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1220">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1221">目标数据库/环境 (target database/environment)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1221">target database/environment</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1222">将程序集及其绑定部署到目标环境时所确定的数据库/环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1222">Identified when deploying an assembly and its bindings into a target environment.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1264">贸易合作伙伴</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1264">trading partner</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1265">与你所在组织交换电子数据的外部或内部组织。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1265">An external or internal organization with which your organization exchanges electronic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1266">例如，贸易合作伙伴可以是提供商、客户或内部部门。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1266">For example, a trading partner could be a supplier, a customer, or an internal department.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1267">贸易合作伙伴协议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1267">trading partner agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1268">两个贸易合作伙伴之间的权威和绑定协议，用于通过特定的业务到业务协议处理消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1268">A definitive and binding agreement between two trading partners for transacting messages over a specific business-to-business protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1269">贸易合作伙伴协议集中了来自两个合作伙伴特定业务配置文件的常见双向消息处理属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1269">A trading partner agreement brings together common bi-directional message processing properties from specific business profiles of both partners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1270">这是控制两个贸易合作伙伴之间业务事务的所有方面的全面集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1270">It is a comprehensive collection of all aspects governing the business transaction between the two trading partners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1271">贸易合作伙伴协议通常源自每个合作伙伴的配置文件，可以自定义并覆盖需要的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1271">The trading partner agreement is typically derived from the profiles of each partner, with the ability to customize and override the required settings.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1272">贸易合作伙伴管理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1272">trading partner management</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1273">对有关合作伙伴、他们的业务以及企业之间的关系/协议的信息进行管理和存储的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1273">The act of managing and storing information about partners, their business, and business-to-business relationships/agreements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1274">增强的贸易合作伙伴管理 (TPM) 解决方案，能够更直观地反映业务实体与关系，据此，组织可以更好地管理与贸易合作伙伴的业务伙伴关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1274">The enhanced trading partner management (TPM) solution more intuitively reflects the business entities and relationships, thereby enabling organizations to better manage business partnerships with trading partners.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1275">贸易参与方</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1275">trading party</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1276">实体是位于根级别的一种贸易合作伙伴管理 (TPM) 解决方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1276">An entity that is at the root level of a trading partner management (TPM) solution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1277">处于持续业务关系中的每一个参与组织，以及运行 BizTalk Server 及发送或接收（来自或发往任何其他参与方的）消息的任何单个的业务实体，都是一个贸易参与方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1277">Each participating organization in an ongoing business relationship, and any single business entity that is running BizTalk Server and sending or receiving messages to or from any other party, is a trading party.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1278">事务消息传送</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1278">transactional messaging</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1279">通过同步和协调一组中多个 BizTalk 消息队列适配器实例，严格按顺序一次性发送一系列消息的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1279">A stream of messages sent in order exactly once, achieved by synchronizing and coordinating multiple BizTalk message queuing adapter instances in a group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1280">转换形状 (Transform shape)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1280">Transform shape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1281">业务流程中用于将数据从一个消息移动到另一个消息，并使用 XSLT 映射对其进行转换的形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1281">A shape in an orchestration that is used to move data from one message into another message, and have it transformed using an XSLT map.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1282">转换</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1282">transformation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1283">将符合某种架构的 XML 文档转换为符合另一种架构的 XML 文档的过程，在此过程中通常会改变文档结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1283">The process of converting an XML document that conforms to one schema into an XML document that conforms to another schema, often changing the document structure in the process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1284">转换 (translation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1284">translation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1285">将 XML 文档转换为本地（非 XML）格式，戓将非 XML 文档转换为 XML 文档的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1285">The process of converting an XML document into native (non-XML) format, or vice versa.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1286">传输协议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1286">transport agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1287">两个贸易合作伙伴的业务配置文件之间的协议，可在交换消息时使用特定的传输协议（AS2）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1287">An agreement between the business profiles of two trading partners to use a specific transport protocol (AS2) while exchanging messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1288">传输层安全性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1288">Transport Layer Security</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1289">一种协议，提供通过网络通信的两个应用程序之间的通信隐私性和安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1289">A protocol that provides communications privacy and security between two applications communicating over a network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1290">TLS 对通信进行加密，并使客户端对服务器进行身份验证，并使（可选）服务器对客户端进行身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1290">TLS encrypts communications and enables clients to authenticate servers and, optionally, servers to authenticate clients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1291">TLS 是安全套接字层 (SSL) 协议的更安全的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1291">TLS is a more secure version of the Secure Sockets Layer (SSL) protocol.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1292">传输协议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1292">transport protocol</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1293">一种协议，可控制用于在两个合作伙伴之间来回发送消息的传输通道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1293">A protocol that governs the transport channel used for sending messages back and forth between two partners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1294">关于贸易合作伙伴管理 (TPM)，只支持 AS2 协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1294">With respect to trading partner management (TPM), only the AS2 protocol is supported.</span></span>|

## <a name="v"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1310">V</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1310">V</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1311">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1311">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1312">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1312">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1313">版本控制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1313">versioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1314">更新项目实现以及增加项目版本号的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1314">The act of updating the implementation of an artifact and incrementing its version number.</span></span>|

## <a name="w"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1321">W</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1321">W</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1322">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1322">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1323">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1323">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1324">Web Services</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1324">Web services</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1325">提供数据和向其他应用程序的服务的应用程序逻辑的单位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1325">A unit of application logic providing data and services to other applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1326">应用程序使用标准 Web 协议和数据格式（如 HTTP、XML 和 SOAP）访问 XML Web Services，并与每个 XML Web Services 如何实现无关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1326">Applications access XML Web services using standard Web protocols and data formats such as HTTP, XML, and SOAP, independent of how each XML Web service is implemented.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1327">XML Web Services 结合了基于组件的开发和 Web 两者的优点，同时还是 Microsoft .NET 编程模型的基础。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1327">XML Web services combine the best aspects of component-based development and the Web, and are a cornerstone of the Microsoft .NET programming model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1328">Web Services 描述语言 (WSDL)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1328">Web Services Description Language (WSDL)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1329">一种 XML 格式的语言，它将 Web Services 描述为用于交换消息的终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1329">An XML-formatted language that describes Web services as endpoints for exchanging messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1330">可对该语言进行扩展，从而不考虑消息格式和网络协议而对终结点及其消息进行描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1330">It is extensible to allow for the description of endpoints and their messages regardless of the message format and network protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1331">该语言是通用描述、发现和集成 (UDDI) 所使用的语言，UDDI 是基于 Web 的业务目录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1331">It is the language used by Universal Description, Discovery, and Integration (UDDI), which is a Web-based business directory.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1332">Windows 管理规范 (WMI)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1332">Windows Management Instrumentation (WMI)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1333">WMI 是 Microsoft Windows 操作系统的一个组件和 Microsoft 基于 Web 的企业管理 (WBEM) 实现方案，用于自动执行企业环境中的管理任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1333">A component of the Microsoft Windows operating system and the Microsoft implementation of Web-Based Enterprise Management (WBEM), used to automate administrative tasks in an enterprise environment.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1334">WMI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1334">WMI</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1335">请参阅揥“Windows 管理规范”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1335">See Windows Management Instrumentation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1336">工作队列 (work queue)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1336">work queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1337">包含要由 BizTalk Server 处理的消息的队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1337">A queue that contains messages to be processed by a BizTalk server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1338">WSDL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1338">WSDL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1339">请参阅揥“Web Services 描述语言”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1339">See Web Services Description Language.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="x"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1340">X</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1340">X</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1341">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1341">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1342">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1342">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1343">X.509 证书 (X.509 certificate)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1343">X.509 certificate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1344">Windows 基于证书的进程所使用的标准证书格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1344">The standard certificate format used by Windows certificate-based processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1345">X.509 证书包含公钥和有关证书的颁发对象（个人或实体）的信息、有关该证书的信息以及有关颁发证书的证书颁发机构 (CA) 的可选信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1345">An X.509 certificate includes the public key and information about the person or entity to whom the certificate is issued, information about the certificate, plus optional information about the certification authority (CA) issuing the certificate.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1346">XDR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1346">XDR</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1347">请参阅“精简 XML 数据”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1347">See XML-Data Reduced.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1348">XML 架构定义语言 (XML Schema definition language, XSD)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1348">XML Schema definition language (XSD)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1349">一种架构语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1349">A schema language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1350">由 XML 架构定义的元素、属性和数据类型符合“万维网联合会 (W3C) XML 架构第 1 部分：针对 XML 架构定义语言的结构建议”的规定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1350">An XML Schema defines the elements, attributes, and data types that conform to the World Wide Web Consortium (W3C) XML Schema Part 1: Structures Recommendation for the XML Schema Definition Language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1351">“W3C XML Schema Part 2: Datatypes Recommendation”是有关如何定义 XML 架构中使用的数据类型的建议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1351">The W3C XML Schema Part 2: Datatypes Recommendation is the recommendation for defining data types used in XML schemas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1352">使用 XML 架构定义语言可以定义 XML 消息的结构和数据类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1352">The XML Schema definition language enables you to define the structure and data types for XML messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1353">精简 XML 数据 (XDR)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1353">XML-Data Reduced (XDR)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1354">描述 XML 文档结构的一种方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1354">One of several ways in which the structure of an XML document can be described.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1355">BizTalk Server 可打开使用 XDR 描述的架构，但是在进程中会将其转换为 XML 架构定义语言 (XSD)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1355">BizTalk Server can open a schema described using XDR, but converts it to XML Schema definition language (XSD) in the process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1356">XPath</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1356">XPath</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1357">一种用于在 XML 文档的分层结构中进行导航的综合语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1357">A comprehensive language used for navigating through the hierarchy of an XML document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1358">XPath 表达式可以包含 XML 元素和属性信息，可以选择符合特定条件的数据，并可以执行检索数据的比较。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1358">XPath expressions can contain XML element and attribute information, select data that matches specific criteria, and perform comparisons on the data retrieved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1359">也称作节点路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1359">Also called a node path.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1360">XSD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1360">XSD</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1361">请参阅揦“XML 架构定义语言”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1361">See XML Schema Definition language.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1362">XSLT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1362">XSLT</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1363">请参阅“可扩展样式表语言转换”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1363">See Extensible Stylesheet Language Transformations.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="z"></a><span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1364">Z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1364">Z</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1365">术语</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1365">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1366">定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1366">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1367">僵停 (zombie)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1367">zombie</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1368">业务流程未处理的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1368">A message that was not processed by an orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1369">它不在“已挂起”队列中，也不在将进行重试的任何其他位置中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1369">It is not in the Suspended queue or anywhere else where it will be retried.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1370">僵停复活 (zombie resurrector)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1370">zombie resurrector</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="d3ae6-1371">一种业务流程，可在 MessageBox 数据库侦听僵停，并复活那些符合特定标准的僵停。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d3ae6-1371">An orchestration that listens at the MessageBox database for zombies and resurrects those that meet certain criteria.</span></span>|
